Through the lives, deaths, tragedies and loves of the Freeman family, the series charts how Britain was shaped after World War II. It was subsequently broadcast in the USA on BBC America. The show was co-financed between WGBH-TV and the BBC and was produced by Michael Riley and John Chapman. Executive Producers were Peter Fincham and Tessa Ross.\n\nThe soundtrack was written by composer and musician Jocelyn Pook.", "poster_path": "/tmEAWh03eNJNEfDhVlAa3eRfxPz.jpg", "media_type": "tv", "adult": false, "original_language": "en", "genre_ids": [18], "popularity": 1.3576, "first_air_date": "2001-01-10", "vote_average": 2.0, "vote_count": 1, "origin_country": ["GB"]}]}]}
